class="item-text">特別企劃</div></a></div></div></div></div></div><style type="text/css">#award-countdown,#award-announced{display:none;font-size:14px}#award-countdown a,#award-announced a{color:#fff038}#award-countdown{padding-left:39px}#award-countdown #countdown{margin-left:5px;margin-right:5px}#award-announced{padding-left:96px}</style><script type="text/javascript">(function() {
  var countdownTimer, seconds, upgradeTime;

  window.timer = function() {
    var days, hours, hoursLeft, minutes, minutesLeft, remainingSeconds;
    days = Math.floor(seconds / 24 / 60 / 60);
    hoursLeft = Math.floor(seconds - (days * 86400));
    hours = Math.floor(hoursLeft / 3600);
    minutesLeft = Math.floor(hoursLeft - (hours * 3600));
    minutes = Math.floor(minutesLeft / 60);
    remainingSeconds = seconds % 60;
    if (hours < 10) {
      hours = '0' + hours;
    }
    if (minutes < 10) {
      minutes = '0' + minutes;
    }
    if (remainingSeconds < 10) {
      remainingSeconds = '0' + remainingSeconds;
    }
    $('#countdown').html(days + '天' + hours + '時' + minutes + '分' + remainingSeconds + '秒');
    if (seconds <= 0) {
      clearInterval(countdownTimer);
      $('#award-countdown').hide();
      $('#award-announced').show();
    } else {
      seconds--;
    }
  };

  upgradeTime = parseInt((new Date(2018, 3, 12, 11, 0, 0, 0) - new Date().getTime()) / 1000);

  seconds = upgradeTime;

  if (seconds > 0) {
    $('#award-countdown').show();
    countdownTimer = setInterval('timer()', 1000);
  } else {
    $('#award-announced').show();
  }

}).call(this);
</script><div class="message-push flash-alert"><div class="message-dialog"><button class="close-message" onclick="closeFlashAlert();" title="Close (Esc)" type="button"> ×</button><div
